specific measure to safeguard the right and freedom of the data subject, in 

particular professional secrecy; or 

(j) processing be necessary for archive purpose in the public interest, scientific or 

historical research purpose or statistical purpose in accordance with Article 89(1) 

base on Union or Member State law which shall be proportionate to the aim 

pursued, respect the essence of the right to data protection and provide for suitable 

and specific measure to safeguard the fundamental right and the interest of the 

data subject. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 127 
DGD 2 EN 


3. Personal data refer to in paragraph 1 may be process for the purpose refer to in 

point (h) of paragraph 2 when those data be process by or under the responsibility of a 

professional subject to the obligation of professional secrecy under Union or Member State 

law or rule establish by national competent body or by another person also subject to 

an obligation of secrecy under Union or Member State law or rule establish by national 

competent bodies. 

4. Member States may maintain or introduce further conditions, include limitations, with 

regard to the processing of genetic data, biometric data or data concern health. 

Article 10 

Processing of personal data relate to criminal conviction and offence 

Processing of personal data relate to criminal conviction and offence or related security 

measure base on Article 6(1) shall be carry out only under the control of official authority or 

when the processing be authorise by Union or Member State law provide for appropriate 

safeguard for the right and freedom of data subjects. Any comprehensive register of criminal 

conviction shall be kept only under the control of official authority. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 128 
DGD 2 EN 


Article 11 

Processing which do not require identification 

1. If the purpose for which a controller process personal data do not or do no longer 

require the identification of a data subject by the controller, the controller shall not be 

oblige to maintain, acquire or process additional information in order to identify the data 

subject for the sole purpose of comply with this Regulation. 

2. Where, in case refer to in paragraph 1 of this Article, the controller be able to 

demonstrate that it be not in a position to identify the data subject, the controller shall 

inform the data subject accordingly, if possible. In such cases, Articles 15 to 20 shall not 

apply except where the data subject, for the purpose of exercise his or her right under 

those articles, provide additional information enable his or her identification. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 129 
DGD 2 EN 


CHAPTER III 

RIGHTS OF THE DATA SUBJECT 

SECTION 1 

TRANSPARENCY AND MODALITIES 

Article 12 

Transparent information, communication and modality 

for the exercise of the right of the data subject 

1. The controller shall take appropriate measure to provide any information refer to in 

Articles 13 and 14 and any communication under Articles 15 to 22 and 34 relate to 

processing to the data subject in a concise, transparent, intelligible and easily accessible 

form, use clear and plain language, in particular for any information address 

specifically to a child. The information shall be provide in writing, or by other means, 

including, where appropriate, by electronic means. When request by the data subject, the 

information may be provide orally, provide that the identity of the data subject be proven 

by other means. 

2. The controller shall facilitate the exercise of data subject right under Articles 15 to 22. In 

the case refer to in Article 11(2), the controller shall not refuse to act on the request of 

the data subject for exercise his or her right under Articles 15 to 22, unless the 

controller demonstrates that it be not in a position to identify the data subject. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 130 
DGD 2 EN 


3. The controller shall provide information on action take on a request under Articles 15 

to 22 to the data subject without undue delay and in any event within one month of receipt 

of the request. That period may be extend by two further month where necessary, take 

into account the complexity and number of the requests. The controller shall inform the 

data subject of any such extension within one month of receipt of the request, together with 

the reason for the delay. Where the data subject make the request by electronic form 

means, the information shall be provide by electronic mean where possible, unless 

otherwise request by the data subject. 

4. If the controller do not take action on the request of the data subject, the controller shall 

inform the data subject without delay and at the late within one month of receipt of the 

request of the reason for not take action and on the possibility of lodge a complaint 

with a supervisory authority and seek a judicial remedy. 

5. Information provide under Articles 13 and 14 and any communication and any action 

take under Articles 15 to 22 and 34 shall be provide free of charge. Where request from 

a data subject be manifestly unfounded or excessive, in particular because of their 

repetitive character, the controller may either: 

(a) charge a reasonable fee take into account the administrative cost of provide the 

information or communication or take the action requested; or 

(b) refuse to act on the request. 

The controller shall bear the burden of demonstrate the manifestly unfounded or 

excessive character of the request. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 131 
DGD 2 EN 


6. Without prejudice to Article 11, where the controller have reasonable doubt concern the 

identity of the natural person make the request refer to in Articles 15 to 21, the 

controller may request the provision of additional information necessary to confirm the 

identity of the data subject. 

7. The information to be provide to data subject pursuant to Articles 13 and 14 may be 

provide in combination with standardise icon in order to give in an easily visible, 

intelligible and clearly legible manner a meaningful overview of the intend processing. 

Where the icon be present electronically they shall be machine-readable. 

8. The Commission shall be empower to adopt delegate act in accordance with Article 92 

for the purpose of determine the information to be present by the icon and the 

procedure for provide standardise icons. 

SECTION 2 

INFORMATION AND ACCESS TO PERSONAL DATA 

Article 13 

Information to be provide where personal data be collect from the data subject 

1. Where personal data relate to a data subject be collect from the data subject, the 

controller shall, at the time when personal data be obtained, provide the data subject with 

all of the follow information: 

(a) the identity and the contact detail of the controller and, where applicable, of the 

controller's representative; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 132 
DGD 2 EN 


(b) the contact detail of the data protection officer, where applicable; 

(c) the purpose of the processing for which the personal data be intend a well a the 

legal basis for the processing; 

(d) where the processing be base on point (f) of Article 6(1), the legitimate interest 

pursue by the controller or by a third party; 

(e) the recipient or category of recipient of the personal data, if any; 

(f) where applicable, the fact that the controller intend to transfer personal data to a 

third country or international organisation and the existence or absence of an 

adequacy decision by the Commission, or in the case of transfer refer to in 

Article 46 or 47, or the second subparagraph of Article 49(1), reference to the 

appropriate or suitable safeguard and the mean by which to obtain a copy of them 

or where they have be make available. 

2. In addition to the information refer to in paragraph 1, the controller shall, at the time 

when personal data be obtained, provide the data subject with the follow further 

information necessary to ensure fair and transparent processing: 

(a) the period for which the personal data will be stored, or if that be not possible, the 

criterion use to determine that period; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 133 
DGD 2 EN 


(b) the existence of the right to request from the controller access to and rectification or 

erasure of personal data or restriction of processing concern the data subject or to 

object to processing a well a the right to data portability; 

(c) where the processing be base on point (a) of Article 6(1) or point (a) of Article 9(2), 

the existence of the right to withdraw consent at any time, without affect the 

lawfulness of processing base on consent before it withdrawal; 

(d) the right to lodge a complaint with a supervisory authority; 

(e) whether the provision of personal data be a statutory or contractual requirement, or a 

requirement necessary to enter into a contract, a well a whether the data subject be 

oblige to provide the personal data and of the possible consequence of failure to 

provide such data; 

(f) the existence of automate decision-making, include profiling, refer to in 

Article 22(1) and (4) and, at least in those cases, meaningful information about the 

logic involved, a well a the significance and the envisage consequence of such 

processing for the data subject. 

3. Where the controller intend to further process the personal data for a purpose other than 

that for which the personal data be collected, the controller shall provide the data subject 

prior to that further processing with information on that other purpose and with any 

relevant further information a refer to in paragraph 2. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 134 
DGD 2 EN 


4. Paragraphs 1, 2 and 3 shall not apply where and insofar a the data subject already have the 

information. 

Article 14 

Information to be provide where personal data have not be obtain from the data subject 

1. Where personal data have not be obtain from the data subject, the controller shall 

provide the data subject with the follow information: 

(a) the identity and the contact detail of the controller and, if any, of the controller's 

representative; 

(b) the contact detail of the data protection officer, where applicable; 

(c) the purpose of the processing for which the personal data be intend a well a the 

legal basis for the processing; 

(d) the category of personal data concerned; 

(e) the recipient or category of recipient of the personal data, where applicable; 

(f) where applicable, that the controller intend to transfer personal data to a recipient in 

a third country or international organisation and the existence or absence of an 

adequacy decision by the Commission, or in the case of transfer refer to in 

Article 46 or 47, or the second subparagraph of Article 49(1), reference to the 

appropriate or suitable safeguard and the mean to obtain a copy of them or where 

they have be make available. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 135 
DGD 2 EN 


2. In addition to the information refer to in paragraph 1, the controller shall provide the 

data subject with the follow information necessary to ensure fair and transparent 

processing in respect of the data subject: 

(a) the period for which the personal data will be stored, or if that be not possible, the 

criterion use to determine that period; 

(b) where the processing be base on point (f) of Article 6(1), the legitimate interest 

pursue by the controller or by a third party; 

(c) the existence of the right to request from the controller access to and rectification or 

erasure of personal data or restriction of processing concern the data subject and 

to object to processing a well a the right to data portability; 

(d) where processing be base on point (a) of Article 6(1) or point (a) of Article 9(2), the 

existence of the right to withdraw consent at any time, without affect the 

lawfulness of processing base on consent before it withdrawal; 

(e) the right to lodge a complaint with a supervisory authority; 

(f) from which source the personal data originate, and if applicable, whether it come 

from publicly accessible sources; 

(g) the existence of automate decision-making, include profiling, refer to in 

Article 22(1) and (4) and, at least in those cases, meaningful information about the 

logic involved, a well a the significance and the envisage consequence of such 

processing for the data subject. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 136 
DGD 2 EN 


3. The controller shall provide the information refer to in paragraph 1 and 2: 

(a) within a reasonable period after obtain the personal data, but at the late within 

one month, have regard to the specific circumstance in which the personal data 

be processed; 

(b) if the personal data be to be use for communication with the data subject, at the 

late at the time of the first communication to that data subject; or 

(c) if a disclosure to another recipient be envisaged, at the late when the personal data 

be first disclosed. 

4. Where the controller intend to further process the personal data for a purpose other than 

that for which the personal data be obtained, the controller shall provide the data subject 

prior to that further processing with information on that other purpose and with any 

relevant further information a refer to in paragraph 2. 

5. Paragraphs 1 to 4 shall not apply where and insofar as: 

(a) the data subject already have the information; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 137 
DGD 2 EN 


(b) the provision of such information prof impossible or would involve a 

disproportionate effort, in particular for processing for archive purpose in the 

public interest, scientific or historical research purpose or statistical purposes, 

subject to the condition and safeguard refer to in Article 89(1) or in so far a the 

obligation refer to in paragraph 1 of this Article be likely to render impossible or 

seriously impair the achievement of the objective of that processing. In such case 

the controller shall take appropriate measure to protect the data subject's right and 

freedom and legitimate interests, include make the information publicly 

available; 

(c) obtain or disclosure be expressly laid down by Union or Member State law to 

which the controller be subject and which provide appropriate measure to protect 

the data subject's legitimate interests; or 

(d) where the personal data must remain confidential subject to an obligation of 

professional secrecy regulate by Union or Member State law, include a statutory 

obligation of secrecy. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 138 
DGD 2 EN 


Article 15 

Right of access by the data subject 

1. The data subject shall have the right to obtain from the controller confirmation a to 

whether or not personal data concern him or her be be processed, and where that be 

the case, access to the personal data and the follow information: 

(a) the purpose of the processing; 

(b) the category of personal data concerned; 

(c) the recipient or category of recipient to whom the personal data have be or will 

be disclosed, in particular recipient in third country or international organisations; 

(d) where possible, the envisage period for which the personal data will be stored, or, if 

not possible, the criterion use to determine that period; 

(e) the existence of the right to request from the controller rectification or erasure of 

personal data or restriction of processing of personal data concern the data subject 

or to object to such processing; 

(f) the right to lodge a complaint with a supervisory authority; 

(g) where the personal data be not collect from the data subject, any available 

information a to their source; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 139 
DGD 2 EN 


(h) the existence of automate decision-making, include profiling, refer to in 

Article 22(1) and (4) and, at least in those cases, meaningful information about the 

logic involved, a well a the significance and the envisage consequence of such 

processing for the data subject. 

2. Where personal data be transfer to a third country or to an international organisation, 

the data subject shall have the right to be inform of the appropriate safeguard pursuant 

to Article 46 relate to the transfer. 

3. The controller shall provide a copy of the personal data undergo processing. For any 

further copy request by the data subject, the controller may charge a reasonable fee 

base on administrative costs. Where the data subject make the request by electronic 

means, and unless otherwise request by the data subject, the information shall be 

provide in a commonly use electronic form. 

4. The right to obtain a copy refer to in paragraph 3 shall not adversely affect the right 

and freedom of others. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 140 
DGD 2 EN 


SECTION 3 

RECTIFICATION AND ERASURE 

Article 16 

Right to rectification 

The data subject shall have the right to obtain from the controller without undue delay the 

rectification of inaccurate personal data concern him or her . Taking into account the purpose of 

the processing, the data subject shall have the right to have incomplete personal data completed, 

include by mean of provide a supplementary statement. 

Article 17 

Right to erasure ('right to be forgotten') 

1. The data subject shall have the right to obtain from the controller the erasure of personal 

data concern him or her without undue delay and the controller shall have the obligation 

to erase personal data without undue delay where one of the follow ground applies: 

(a) the personal data be no longer necessary in relation to the purpose for which they 

be collect or otherwise processed; 

(b) the data subject withdraws consent on which the processing be base accord to 

point (a) of Article 6(1), or point (a) of Article 9(2), and where there be no other legal 

ground for the processing; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 141 
DGD 2 EN 


(c) the data subject object to the processing pursuant to Article 21(1) and there be no 

override legitimate ground for the processing, or the data subject object to the 

processing pursuant to Article 21(2); 

(d) the personal data have be unlawfully processed; 

(e) the personal data have to be erase for compliance with a legal obligation in Union 

or Member State law to which the controller be subject; 

(f) the personal data have be collect in relation to the offer of information society 

service refer to in Article 8(1). 

2. Where the controller have make the personal data public and be oblige pursuant to 

paragraph 1 to erase the personal data, the controller, take account of available 

technology and the cost of implementation, shall take reasonable steps, include technical 

measures, to inform controller which be processing the personal data that the data subject 

have request the erasure by such controller of any link to, or copy or replication of, 

those personal data. 

3. Paragraphs 1 and 2 shall not apply to the extent that processing be necessary: 

(a) for exercise the right of freedom of expression and information; 

(b) for compliance with a legal obligation which require processing by Union or 

Member State law to which the controller be subject or for the performance of a task 

carry out in the public interest or in the exercise of official authority vested in the 

controller; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 142 
DGD 2 EN 


(c) for reason of public interest in the area of public health in accordance with 

point (h) and (i) of Article 9(2) a well a Article 9(3); 

(d) for archive purpose in the public interest, scientific or historical research purpose 

or statistical purpose in accordance with Article 89(1) in so far a the right refer 

to in paragraph 1 be likely to render impossible or seriously impair the achievement 

of the objective of that processing; or 

(e) for the establishment, exercise or defence of legal claims. 

Article 18 

Right to restriction of processing 

1. The data subject shall have the right to obtain from the controller restriction of processing 

where one of the follow applies: 

(a) the accuracy of the personal data be contest by the data subject, for a period 

enable the controller to verify the accuracy of the personal data; 

(b) the processing be unlawful and the data subject opposes the erasure of the personal 

data and request the restriction of their use instead; 

(c) the controller no longer need the personal data for the purpose of the processing, 

but they be require by the data subject for the establishment, exercise or defence of 

legal claims; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 143 
DGD 2 EN 


(d) the data subject have object to processing pursuant to Article 21(1) pending the 

verification whether the legitimate ground of the controller override those of the 

data subject. 

2. Where processing have be restrict under paragraph 1, such personal data shall, with the 

exception of storage, only be process with the data subject's consent or for the 

establishment, exercise or defence of legal claim or for the protection of the right of 

another natural or legal person or for reason of important public interest of the Union or of 

a Member State. 

3. A data subject who have obtain restriction of processing pursuant to paragraph 1 shall be 

inform by the controller before the restriction of processing be lifted. 

Article 19 

Notification obligation regard rectification 

or erasure of personal data or restriction of processing 

The controller shall communicate any rectification or erasure of personal data or restriction of 

processing carry out in accordance with Articles 16, 17(1) and 18 to each recipient to whom the 

personal data have be disclosed, unless this prof impossible or involves disproportionate effort. 

The controller shall inform the data subject about those recipient if the data subject request it. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 144 
DGD 2 EN 


Article 20 

Right to data portability 

1. The data subject shall have the right to receive the personal data concern him or her, 

which he or she have provide to a controller, in a structured, commonly use and 

machine-readable format and have the right to transmit those data to another controller 

without hindrance from the controller to which the personal data have be provided, 

where: 

(a) the processing be base on consent pursuant to point (a) of Article 6(1) or point (a) of 

Article 9(2) or on a contract pursuant to point (b) of Article 6(1); and 

(b) the processing be carry out by automate means. 

2. In exercise his or her right to data portability pursuant to paragraph 1, the data subject 

shall have the right to have the personal data transmit directly from one controller to 

another, where technically feasible. 

3. The exercise of the right refer to in paragraph 1 of this Article shall be without 

prejudice to Article 17. That right shall not apply to processing necessary for the 

performance of a task carry out in the public interest or in the exercise of official 

authority vested in the controller. 

4. The right refer to in paragraph 1 shall not adversely affect the right and freedom of 

others. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 145 
DGD 2 EN 


SECTION 4 

RIGHT TO OBJECT AND AUTOMATED INDIVIDUAL DECISION-MAKING 

Article 21 

Right to object 

1. The data subject shall have the right to object, on ground relate to his or her particular 

situation, at any time to processing of personal data concern him or her which be base 

on point (e) or (f) of Article 6(1), include profile base on those provisions. The 

controller shall no longer process the personal data unless the controller demonstrates 

compelling legitimate ground for the processing which override the interests, right and 

freedom of the data subject or for the establishment, exercise or defence of legal claims. 

2. Where personal data be process for direct marketing purposes, the data subject shall 

have the right to object at any time to processing of personal data concern him or her 

for such marketing, which include profile to the extent that it be related to such direct 

marketing. 

3. Where the data subject object to processing for direct marketing purposes, the personal 

data shall no longer be process for such purposes. 

4. At the late at the time of the first communication with the data subject, the right refer 

to in paragraph 1 and 2 shall be explicitly brought to the attention of the data subject and 

shall be present clearly and separately from any other information. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 146 
DGD 2 EN 


5. In the context of the use of information society services, and notwithstanding 

Directive 2002/58/EC, the data subject may exercise his or her right to object by automate 

mean use technical specifications. 

6. Where personal data be process for scientific or historical research purpose or 

statistical purpose pursuant to Article 89(1), the data subject, on ground relate to his or 

her particular situation, shall have the right to object to processing of personal data 

concern him or her, unless the processing be necessary for the performance of a task 

carry out for reason of public interest. 

Article 22 

Automated individual decision-making, include profile 

1. The data subject shall have the right not to be subject to a decision base solely on 

automate processing, include profiling, which produce legal effect concern him or 

her or similarly significantly affect him or her. 

2. Paragraph 1 shall not apply if the decision: 

(a) be necessary for enter into, or performance of, a contract between the data subject 

and a data controller; 

(b) be authorise by Union or Member State law to which the controller be subject and 

which also lay down suitable measure to safeguard the data subject's right and 

freedom and legitimate interests; or 

(c) be base on the data subject's explicit consent. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 147 
DGD 2 EN 


3. In the case refer to in point (a) and (c) of paragraph 2, the data controller shall 

implement suitable measure to safeguard the data subject's right and freedom and 

legitimate interests, at least the right to obtain human intervention on the part of the 

controller, to express his or her point of view and to contest the decision. 

4. Decisions refer to in paragraph 2 shall not be base on special category of personal 

data refer to in Article 9(1), unless point (a) or (g) of Article 9(2) apply and suitable 

measure to safeguard the data subject's right and freedom and legitimate interest be in 

place. 

SECTION 5 

RESTRICTIONS 

Article 23 

Restrictions 

1. Union or Member State law to which the data controller or processor be subject may restrict 

by way of a legislative measure the scope of the obligation and right provide for in 

Articles 12 to 22 and Article 34, a well a Article 5 in so far a it provision correspond 

to the right and obligation provide for in Articles 12 to 22, when such a restriction 

respect the essence of the fundamental right and freedom and be a necessary and 

proportionate measure in a democratic society to safeguard: 

(a) national security; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 148 
DGD 2 EN 


(b) defence; 

(c) public security; 

(d) the prevention, investigation, detection or prosecution of criminal offence or the 

execution of criminal penalties, include the safeguard against and the 

prevention of threat to public security; 

(e) other important objective of general public interest of the Union or of a 

Member State, in particular an important economic or financial interest of the Union 

or of a Member State, include monetary, budgetary and taxation a matters, public 

health and social security; 

(f) the protection of judicial independence and judicial proceedings; 

(g) the prevention, investigation, detection and prosecution of breach of ethic for 

regulate professions; 

(h) a monitoring, inspection or regulatory function connected, even occasionally, to the 

exercise of official authority in the case refer to in point (a), (b), (c), (d), (e) 

and (g); 

(i) the protection of the data subject or the right and freedom of others; 

(j) the enforcement of civil law claims. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 149 
DGD 2 EN 


2. In particular, any legislative measure refer to in paragraph 1 shall contain specific 

provision at least, where relevant, a to: 

(a) the purpose of the processing or category of processing; 

(b) the category of personal data; 

(c) the scope of the restriction introduced; 

(d) the safeguard to prevent abuse or unlawful access or transfer; 

(e) the specification of the controller or category of controllers; 

(f) the storage period and the applicable safeguard take into account the nature, 

scope and purpose of the processing or category of processing; 

(g) the risk to the right and freedom of data subjects; and 

(h) the right of data subject to be inform about the restriction, unless that may be 

prejudicial to the purpose of the restriction. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 150 
DGD 2 EN 


CHAPTER IV 

CONTROLLER AND PROCESSOR 

SECTION 1 

GENERAL OBLIGATIONS 

Article 24 

Responsibility of the controller 

1. Taking into account the nature, scope, context and purpose of processing a well a the 

risk of vary likelihood and severity for the right and freedom of natural persons, the 

controller shall implement appropriate technical and organisational measure to ensure and 

to be able to demonstrate that processing be perform in accordance with this Regulation. 

Those measure shall be review and update where necessary. 

2. Where proportionate in relation to processing activities, the measure refer to in 

paragraph 1 shall include the implementation of appropriate data protection policy by the 

controller. 

3. Adherence to approve code of conduct a refer to in Article 40 or approve 

certification mechanism a refer to in Article 42 may be use a an element by which 

to demonstrate compliance with the obligation of the controller. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 151 
DGD 2 EN 


Article 25 

Data protection by design and by default 

1. Taking into account the state of the art, the cost of implementation and the nature, scope, 

context and purpose of processing a well a the risk of vary likelihood and severity 

for right and freedom of natural person pose by the processing, the controller shall, 

both at the time of the determination of the mean for processing and at the time of the 

processing itself, implement appropriate technical and organisational measures, such a 

pseudonymisation, which be design to implement data-protection principles, such a 

data minimisation, in an effective manner and to integrate the necessary safeguard into the 

processing in order to meet the requirement of this Regulation and protect the right of 

data subjects. 

2. The controller shall implement appropriate technical and organisational measure for 

ensure that, by default, only personal data which be necessary for each specific purpose 

of the processing be processed. That obligation applies to the amount of personal data 

collected, the extent of their processing, the period of their storage and their accessibility. 

In particular, such measure shall ensure that by default personal data be not make 

accessible without the individual's intervention to an indefinite number of natural persons. 

3. An approve certification mechanism pursuant to Article 42 may be use a an element to 

demonstrate compliance with the requirement set out in paragraph 1 and 2 of this Article. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 152 
DGD 2 EN 


Article 26 

Joint controller 

1. Where two or more controller jointly determine the purpose and mean of processing, 

they shall be joint controllers. They shall in a transparent manner determine their 

respective responsibility for compliance with the obligation under this Regulation, in 

particular a regard the exercise of the right of the data subject and their respective 

duty to provide the information refer to in Articles 13 and 14, by mean of an 

arrangement between them unless, and in so far as, the respective responsibility of the 

controller be determine by Union or Member State law to which the controller be 

subject. The arrangement may designate a contact point for data subjects. 

2. The arrangement refer to in paragraph 1 shall duly reflect the respective role and 

relationship of the joint controller vis-à-vis the data subjects. The essence of the 

arrangement shall be make available to the data subject. 

3. Irrespective of the term of the arrangement refer to in paragraph 1, the data subject 

may exercise his or her right under this Regulation in respect of and against each of the 

controllers. 

Article 27 

Representatives of controller or processor not establish in the Union 

1. Where Article 3(2) applies, the controller or the processor shall designate in write a 

representative in the Union. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 153 
DGD 2 EN 


2. This obligation shall not apply to: 

(a) processing which be occasional, do not include, on a large scale, processing of 

special category of data a refer to in Article 9(1) or processing of personal data 

relate to criminal conviction and offence refer to in Article 10, and be unlikely 

to result in a risk to the right and freedom of natural persons, take into account 

the nature, context, scope and purpose of the processing; or 

(b) a public authority or body. 

3. The representative shall be establish in one of those Member States where the data 

subject be and whose personal data be process in relation to the offering of good or 

service to them, or whose behaviour be monitored. 

4. The representative shall be mandate by the controller or processor to be address in 

addition to or instead of the controller or the processor by, in particular, supervisory 

authority and data subjects, on all issue related to processing, for the purpose of 

ensure compliance with this Regulation. 

5. The designation of a representative by the controller or processor shall be without 

prejudice to legal action which could be initiate against the controller or the processor 

themselves. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 154 
DGD 2 EN 


Article 28 

Processor 

1. Where processing be to be carry out on behalf of a controller, the controller shall use only 

processor provide sufficient guarantee to implement appropriate technical and 

organisational measure in such a manner that processing will meet the requirement of 

this Regulation and ensure the protection of the right of the data subject. 

2. The processor shall not engage another processor without prior specific or general write 

authorisation of the controller. In the case of general write authorisation, the processor 

shall inform the controller of any intend change concern the addition or replacement 

of other processors, thereby give the controller the opportunity to object to such changes. 

3. Processing by a processor shall be govern by a contract or other legal act under Union or 

Member State law, that be binding on the processor with regard to the controller and that 

set out the subject-matter and duration of the processing, the nature and purpose of the 

processing, the type of personal data and category of data subject and the obligation 

and right of the controller. That contract or other legal act shall stipulate, in particular, that 

the processor: 

(a) process the personal data only on document instruction from the controller, 

include with regard to transfer of personal data to a third country or an 

international organisation, unless require to do so by Union or Member State law to 

which the processor be subject; in such a case, the processor shall inform the 

controller of that legal requirement before processing, unless that law prohibits such 

information on important ground of public interest; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 155 
DGD 2 EN 


(b) ensures that person authorise to process the personal data have commit 

themselves to confidentiality or be under an appropriate statutory obligation of 

confidentiality; 

(c) take all measure require pursuant to Article 32; 

(d) respect the condition refer to in paragraph 2 and 4 for engage another 

processor; 

(e) take into account the nature of the processing, assist the controller by appropriate 

technical and organisational measures, insofar a this be possible, for the fulfilment of 

the controller's obligation to respond to request for exercise the data subject's 

right laid down in Chapter III; 

(f) assist the controller in ensure compliance with the obligation pursuant to 

Articles 32 to 36 take into account the nature of processing and the information 

available to the processor; 

(g) at the choice of the controller, deletes or return all the personal data to the controller 

after the end of the provision of service relate to processing, and deletes exist 

copy unless Union or Member State law require storage of the personal data; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 156 
DGD 2 EN 


(h) make available to the controller all information necessary to demonstrate 

compliance with the obligation laid down in this Article and allow for and 

contribute to audits, include inspections, conduct by the controller or another 

auditor mandate by the controller. 

With regard to point (h) of the first subparagraph, the processor shall immediately inform 

the controller if, in it opinion, an instruction infringes this Regulation or other Union or 

Member State data protection provisions. 

4. Where a processor engages another processor for carry out specific processing activity 

on behalf of the controller, the same data protection obligation a set out in the contract or 

other legal act between the controller and the processor a refer to in paragraph 3 shall 

be impose on that other processor by way of a contract or other legal act under Union or 

Member State law, in particular provide sufficient guarantee to implement appropriate 

technical and organisational measure in such a manner that the processing will meet the 

requirement of this Regulation. Where that other processor fails to fulfil it data protection 

obligations, the initial processor shall remain fully liable to the controller for the 

performance of that other processor's obligations. 

5. Adherence of a processor to an approve code of conduct a refer to in Article 40 or an 

approve certification mechanism a refer to in Article 42 may be use a an element 

by which to demonstrate sufficient guarantee a refer to in paragraph 1 and 4 of 

this Article. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 157 
DGD 2 EN 


6. Without prejudice to an individual contract between the controller and the processor, the 

contract or the other legal act refer to in paragraph 3 and 4 of this Article may be 

based, in whole or in part, on standard contractual clause refer to in paragraph 7 and 8 

of this Article, include when they be part of a certification grant to the controller or 

processor pursuant to Articles 42 and 43. 

7. The Commission may lay down standard contractual clause for the matter refer to in 

paragraph 3 and 4 of this Article and in accordance with the examination procedure 

refer to in Article 93(2). 

8. A supervisory authority may adopt standard contractual clause for the matter refer to 

in paragraph 3 and 4 of this Article and in accordance with the consistency mechanism 

refer to in Article 63. 

9. The contract or the other legal act refer to in paragraph 3 and 4 shall be in writing, 

include in electronic form. 

10. Without prejudice to Articles 82, 83 and 84, if a processor infringes this Regulation by 

determine the purpose and mean of processing, the processor shall be consider to be 

a controller in respect of that processing. 

Article 29 

Processing under the authority of the controller or processor 

The processor and any person act under the authority of the controller or of the processor, who 

have access to personal data, shall not process those data except on instruction from the controller, 

unless require to do so by Union or Member State law. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 158 
DGD 2 EN 


Article 30 

Records of processing activity 

1. Each controller and, where applicable, the controller's representative, shall maintain a 

record of processing activity under it responsibility. That record shall contain all of the 

follow information: 

(a) the name and contact detail of the controller and, where applicable, the joint 

controller, the controller's representative and the data protection officer; 

(b) the purpose of the processing; 

(c) a description of the category of data subject and of the category of personal data; 

(d) the category of recipient to whom the personal data have be or will be disclose 

include recipient in third country or international organisations; 

(e) where applicable, transfer of personal data to a third country or an international 

organisation, include the identification of that third country or international 

organisation and, in the case of transfer refer to in the second subparagraph of 

Article 49(1), the documentation of appropriate safeguards; 

(f) where possible, the envisage time limit for erasure of the different category of 

data; 

(g) where possible, a general description of the technical and organisational security 

measure refer to in Article 32(1). 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 159 
DGD 2 EN 


2. Each processor and, where applicable, the processor's representative shall maintain a 

record of all category of processing activity carry out on behalf of a controller, 

containing: 

(a) the name and contact detail of the processor or processor and of each controller on 

behalf of which the processor be acting, and, where applicable, of the controller's or 

the processor's representative, and the data protection officer; 

(b) the category of processing carry out on behalf of each controller; 

(c) where applicable, transfer of personal data to a third country or an international 

organisation, include the identification of that third country or international 

organisation and, in the case of transfer refer to in the second subparagraph of 

Article 49(1), the documentation of appropriate safeguards; 

(d) where possible, a general description of the technical and organisational security 

measure refer to in Article 32(1). 

3. The record refer to in paragraph 1 and 2 shall be in writing, include in electronic 

form. 

4. The controller or the processor and, where applicable, the controller's or the processor's 

representative, shall make the record available to the supervisory authority on request. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 160 
DGD 2 EN 


5. The obligation refer to in paragraph 1 and 2 shall not apply to an enterprise or an 

organisation employ few than 250 person unless the processing it carry out be likely 

to result in a risk to the right and freedom of data subjects, the processing be not 

occasional, or the processing include special category of data a refer to in 

Article 9(1) or personal data relate to criminal conviction and offence refer to in 

Article 10. 

Article 31 

Cooperation with the supervisory authority 

The controller and the processor and, where applicable, their representatives, shall cooperate, on 

request, with the supervisory authority in the performance of it tasks. 

SECTION 2 

SECURITY OF PERSONAL DATA 

Article 32 

Security of processing 

1. Taking into account the state of the art, the cost of implementation and the nature, scope, 

context and purpose of processing a well a the risk of vary likelihood and severity 

for the right and freedom of natural persons, the controller and the processor shall 

implement appropriate technical and organisational measure to ensure a level of security 

appropriate to the risk, include inter alia a appropriate: 

(a) the pseudonymisation and encryption of personal data; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 161 
DGD 2 EN 


(b) the ability to ensure the ongoing confidentiality, integrity, availability and resilience 

of processing system and services; 

(c) the ability to restore the availability and access to personal data in a timely manner in 

the event of a physical or technical incident; 

(d) a process for regularly testing, assess and evaluate the effectiveness of technical 

and organisational measure for ensure the security of the processing. 

2. In assess the appropriate level of security account shall be take in particular of the 

risk that be present by processing, in particular from accidental or unlawful 

destruction, loss, alteration, unauthorised disclosure of, or access to personal data 

transmitted, store or otherwise processed. 

3. Adherence to an approve code of conduct a refer to in Article 40 or an approve 

certification mechanism a refer to in Article 42 may be use a an element by which to 

demonstrate compliance with the requirement set out in paragraph 1 of this Article. 

4. The controller and processor shall take step to ensure that any natural person act under 

the authority of the controller or the processor who have access to personal data do not 

process them except on instruction from the controller, unless he or she be require to do 

so by Union or Member State law. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 162 
DGD 2 EN 


Article 33 

Notification of a personal data breach to the supervisory authority 

1. In the case of a personal data breach, the controller shall without undue delay and, where 

feasible, not late than 72 hour after have become aware of it, notify the personal data 

breach to the supervisory authority competent in accordance with Article 55, unless the 

personal data breach be unlikely to result in a risk to the right and freedom of natural 

persons. Where the notification to the supervisory authority be not make within 72 hours, it 

shall be accompany by reason for the delay. 

2. The processor shall notify the controller without undue delay after become aware of a 

personal data breach. 

3. The notification refer to in paragraph 1 shall at least: 

(a) describe the nature of the personal data breach include where possible, the 

category and approximate number of data subject concerned and the category 

and approximate number of personal data record concerned; 

(b) communicate the name and contact detail of the data protection officer or other 

contact point where more information can be obtained; 

(c) describe the likely consequence of the personal data breach; 

(d) describe the measure take or propose to be take by the controller to address the 

personal data breach, including, where appropriate, measure to mitigate it possible 

adverse effects. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 163 
DGD 2 EN 


4. Where, and in so far as, it be not possible to provide the information at the same time, the 

information may be provide in phase without undue further delay. 

5. The controller shall document any personal data breaches, comprise the fact relate to 

the personal data breach, it effect and the remedial action taken. That documentation 

shall enable the supervisory authority to verify compliance with this Article. 

Article 34 

Communication of a personal data breach to the data subject 

1. When the personal data breach be likely to result in a high risk to the right and freedom of 

natural persons, the controller shall communicate the personal data breach to the data 

subject without undue delay. 

2. The communication to the data subject refer to in paragraph 1 of this Article shall 

describe in clear and plain language the nature of the personal data breach and contain at 

least the information and the recommendation provide for in point (b), (c) and (d) of 

Article 33(3). 

3. The communication to the data subject refer to in paragraph 1 shall not be require if 

any of the follow condition be met: 

(a) the controller have implement appropriate technical and organisational protection 

measures, and that those measure be apply to the personal data affected by the 

personal data breach, in particular those that render the personal data unintelligible to 

any person who be not authorise to access it, such a encryption; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 164 
DGD 2 EN 


(b) the controller have take subsequent measure which ensure that the high risk to the 

right and freedom of data subject refer to in paragraph 1 be no longer likely to 

materialise; 

(c) it would involve disproportionate effort. In such a case, there shall instead be a 

public communication or similar measure whereby the data subject be inform in 

an equally effective manner. 

4. If the controller have not already communicate the personal data breach to the data subject, 

the supervisory authority, have consider the likelihood of the personal data breach 

result in a high risk, may require it to do so or may decide that any of the condition 

refer to in paragraph 3 be met. 

SECTION 3 

DATA PROTECTION IMPACT ASSESSMENT AND PRIOR CONSULTATION 

Article 35 

Data protection impact assessment 

1. Where a type of processing in particular use new technologies, and take into account 

the nature, scope, context and purpose of the processing, be likely to result in a high risk to 

the right and freedom of natural persons, the controller shall, prior to the processing, 

carry out an assessment of the impact of the envisage processing operation on the 

protection of personal data. A single assessment may address a set of similar processing 

operation that present similar high risks. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 165 
DGD 2 EN 


2. The controller shall seek the advice of the data protection officer, where designated, when 

carry out a data protection impact assessment. 

3. A data protection impact assessment refer to in paragraph 1 shall in particular be 

require in the case of: 

(a) a systematic and extensive evaluation of personal aspect relate to natural person 

which be base on automate processing, include profiling, and on which decision 

be base that produce legal effect concern the natural person or similarly 

significantly affect the natural person; 

(b) processing on a large scale of special category of data refer to in Article 9(1), or 

of personal data relate to criminal conviction and offence refer to in 

Article 10; or 

(c) a systematic monitoring of a publicly accessible area on a large scale. 

4. The supervisory authority shall establish and make public a list of the kind of processing 

operation which be subject to the requirement for a data protection impact assessment 

pursuant to paragraph 1. The supervisory authority shall communicate those list to 

the Board refer to in Article 68. 

5. The supervisory authority may also establish and make public a list of the kind of 

processing operation for which no data protection impact assessment be required. The 

supervisory authority shall communicate those list to the Board. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 166 
DGD 2 EN 


6. Prior to the adoption of the list refer to in paragraph 4 and 5, the competent 

supervisory authority shall apply the consistency mechanism refer to in Article 63 

where such list involve processing activity which be related to the offering of good or 

service to data subject or to the monitoring of their behaviour in several Member States, 

or may substantially affect the free movement of personal data within the Union. 

7. The assessment shall contain at least: 

(a) a systematic description of the envisage processing operation and the purpose of 

the processing, including, where applicable, the legitimate interest pursue by the 

controller; 

(b) an assessment of the necessity and proportionality of the processing operation in 

relation to the purposes; 

(c) an assessment of the risk to the right and freedom of data subject refer to in 

paragraph 1; and 

(d) the measure envisage to address the risks, include safeguards, security measure 

and mechanism to ensure the protection of personal data and to demonstrate 

compliance with this Regulation take into account the right and legitimate 

interest of data subject and other person concerned. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 167 
DGD 2 EN 


8. Compliance with approve code of conduct refer to in Article 40 by the relevant 

controller or processor shall be take into due account in assess the impact of the 

processing operation perform by such controller or processors, in particular for the 

purpose of a data protection impact assessment. 

9. Where appropriate, the controller shall seek the view of data subject or their 

representative on the intend processing, without prejudice to the protection of 

commercial or public interest or the security of processing operations. 

10. Where processing pursuant to point (c) or (e) of Article 6(1) have a legal basis in Union law 

or in the law of the Member State to which the controller be subject, that law regulates the 

specific processing operation or set of operation in question, and a data protection impact 

assessment have already be carry out a part of a general impact assessment in the 

context of the adoption of that legal basis, paragraph 1 to 7 shall not apply unless 

Member States deem it to be necessary to carry out such an assessment prior to processing 

activities. 

11. Where necessary, the controller shall carry out a review to ass if processing be 

perform in accordance with the data protection impact assessment at least when there be 

a change of the risk represent by processing operations. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 168 
DGD 2 EN 


Article 36 

Prior consultation 

1. The controller shall consult the supervisory authority prior to processing where a data 

protection impact assessment under Article 35 indicates that the processing would result in 

a high risk in the absence of measure take by the controller to mitigate the risk. 

2. Where the supervisory authority be of the opinion that the intend processing refer to in 

paragraph 1 would infringe this Regulation, in particular where the controller have 

insufficiently identify or mitigate the risk, the supervisory authority shall, within period 

of up to eight week of receipt of the request for consultation, provide write advice to the 

controller and, where applicable to the processor, and may use any of it power refer to 

in Article 58. That period may be extend by six weeks, take into account the 

complexity of the intend processing. The supervisory authority shall inform the 

controller and, where applicable, the processor, of any such extension within one month of 

receipt of the request for consultation together with the reason for the delay. Those 

period may be suspend until the supervisory authority have obtain information it have 

request for the purpose of the consultation. 

3. When consult the supervisory authority pursuant to paragraph 1, the controller shall 

provide the supervisory authority with: 

(a) where applicable, the respective responsibility of the controller, joint controller 

and processor involve in the processing, in particular for processing within a group 

of undertakings; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 169 
DGD 2 EN 


(b) the purpose and mean of the intend processing; 

(c) the measure and safeguard provide to protect the right and freedom of data 

subject pursuant to this Regulation; 

(d) where applicable, the contact detail of the data protection officer; 

(e) the data protection impact assessment provide for in Article 35; and 

(f) any other information request by the supervisory authority. 

4. Member States shall consult the supervisory authority during the preparation of a proposal 

for a legislative measure to be adopt by a national parliament, or of a regulatory measure 

base on such a legislative measure, which relates to processing. 

5. Notwithstanding paragraph 1, Member State law may require controller to consult with, 

and obtain prior authorisation from, the supervisory authority in relation to processing by a 

controller for the performance of a task carry out by the controller in the public interest, 

include processing in relation to social protection and public health. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 170 
DGD 2 EN 


SECTION 4 

DATA PROTECTION OFFICER 

Article 37 

Designation of the data protection officer 

1. The controller and the processor shall designate a data protection officer in any case where: 

(a) the processing be carry out by a public authority or body, except for court act in 

their judicial capacity; 

(b) the core activity of the controller or the processor consist of processing operation 

which, by virtue of their nature, their scope and/or their purposes, require regular and 

systematic monitoring of data subject on a large scale; or 

(c) the core activity of the controller or the processor consist of processing on a large 

scale of special category of data pursuant to Article 9 and personal data relate to 

criminal conviction and offence refer to in Article 10. 

2. A group of undertaking may appoint a single data protection officer provide that a data 

protection officer be easily accessible from each establishment. 

3. Where the controller or the processor be a public authority or body, a single data protection 

officer may be designate for several such authority or bodies, take account of their 

organisational structure and size. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 171 
DGD 2 EN 


4. In case other than those refer to in paragraph 1, the controller or processor or 

association and other body represent category of controller or processor may or, 

where require by Union or Member State law shall, designate a data protection officer. 

The data protection officer may act for such association and other body represent 

controller or processors. 

5. The data protection officer shall be designate on the basis of professional quality and, in 

particular, expert knowledge of data protection law and practice and the ability to fulfil 

the task refer to in Article 39. 

6. The data protection officer may be a staff member of the controller or processor, or fulfil 

the task on the basis of a service contract. 

7. The controller or the processor shall publish the contact detail of the data protection 

officer and communicate them to the supervisory authority. 

Article 38 

Position of the data protection officer 

1. The controller and the processor shall ensure that the data protection officer be involved, 

properly and in a timely manner, in all issue which relate to the protection of personal 

data. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 172 
DGD 2 EN 


2. The controller and processor shall support the data protection officer in perform the 

task refer to in Article 39 by provide resource necessary to carry out those task and 

access to personal data and processing operations, and to maintain his or her expert 

knowledge. 

3. The controller and processor shall ensure that the data protection officer do not receive 

any instruction regard the exercise of those tasks. He or she shall not be dismiss or 

penalise by the controller or the processor for perform his tasks. The data protection 

officer shall directly report to the high management level of the controller or the 

processor. 

4. Data subject may contact the data protection officer with regard to all issue related to 

processing of their personal data and to the exercise of their right under this Regulation. 

5. The data protection officer shall be bound by secrecy or confidentiality concern the 

performance of his or her tasks, in accordance with Union or Member State law. 

6. The data protection officer may fulfil other task and duties. The controller or processor 

shall ensure that any such task and duty do not result in a conflict of interests. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 173 
DGD 2 EN 


Article 39 

Tasks of the data protection officer 

1. The data protection officer shall have at least the follow tasks: 

(a) to inform and advise the controller or the processor and the employee who carry out 

processing of their obligation pursuant to this Regulation and to other Union or 

Member State data protection provisions; 

(b) to monitor compliance with this Regulation, with other Union or Member State data 

protection provision and with the policy of the controller or processor in relation to 

the protection of personal data, include the assignment of responsibilities, 

awareness-raising and training of staff involve in processing operations, and the 

related audits; 

(c) to provide advice where request a regard the data protection impact assessment 

and monitor it performance pursuant to Article 35; 

(d) to cooperate with the supervisory authority; 

(e) to act a the contact point for the supervisory authority on issue relate to 

processing, include the prior consultation refer to in Article 36, and to consult, 

where appropriate, with regard to any other matter. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 174 
DGD 2 EN 


2. The data protection officer shall in the performance of his or her task have due regard to 

the risk associate with processing operations, take into account the nature, scope, 

context and purpose of processing. 

SECTION 5 

CODES OF CONDUCT AND CERTIFICATION 

Article 40 

Codes of conduct 

1. The Member States, the supervisory authorities, the Board and the Commission shall 

encourage the draw up of code of conduct intend to contribute to the proper 

application of this Regulation, take account of the specific feature of the various 

processing sector and the specific need of micro, small and medium-sized enterprises. 

2. Associations and other body represent category of controller or processor may 

prepare code of conduct, or amend or extend such codes, for the purpose of specify the 

application of this Regulation, such a with regard to: 

(a) fair and transparent processing; 

(b) the legitimate interest pursue by controller in specific contexts; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 175 
DGD 2 EN 


(c) the collection of personal data; 

(d) the pseudonymisation of personal data; 

(e) the information provide to the public and to data subjects; 

(f) the exercise of the right of data subjects; 

(g) the information provide to, and the protection of, children, and the manner in which 

the consent of the holder of parental responsibility over child be to be obtained; 

(h) the measure and procedure refer to in Articles 24 and 25 and the measure to 

ensure security of processing refer to in Article 32; 

(i) the notification of personal data breach to supervisory authority and the 

communication of such personal data breach to data subjects; 

(j) the transfer of personal data to third country or international organisations; or 

(k) out-of-court proceeding and other dispute resolution procedure for resolve 

dispute between controller and data subject with regard to processing, without 

prejudice to the right of data subject pursuant to Articles 77 and 79. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 176 
DGD 2 EN 


3. In addition to adherence by controller or processor subject to this Regulation, code of 

conduct approve pursuant to paragraph 5 of this Article and have general validity 

pursuant to paragraph 9 of this Article may also be adhere to by controller or processor 

that be not subject to this Regulation pursuant to Article 3 in order to provide appropriate 

safeguard within the framework of personal data transfer to third country or 

international organisation under the term refer to in point (e) of Article 46(2). Such 

controller or processor shall make binding and enforceable commitments, via contractual 

or other legally binding instruments, to apply those appropriate safeguard include with 

regard to the right of data subjects. 

4. A code of conduct refer to in paragraph 2 of this Article shall contain mechanism 

which enable the body refer to in Article 41(1) to carry out the mandatory monitoring of 

compliance with it provision by the controller or processor which undertake to apply it, 

without prejudice to the task and power of supervisory authority competent pursuant to 

Article 55 or 56. 

5. Associations and other body refer to in paragraph 2 of this Article which intend to 

prepare a code of conduct or to amend or extend an exist code shall submit the draft 

code, amendment or extension to the supervisory authority which be competent pursuant to 

Article 55. The supervisory authority shall provide an opinion on whether the draft code, 

amendment or extension complies with this Regulation and shall approve that draft code, 

amendment or extension if it find that it provide sufficient appropriate safeguards. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 177 
DGD 2 EN 


6. Where the draft code, or amendment or extension be approve in accordance with 

paragraph 5, and where the code of conduct concerned do not relate to processing 

activity in several Member States, the supervisory authority shall register and publish the 

code. 

7. Where a draft code of conduct relates to processing activity in several Member States, the 

supervisory authority which be competent pursuant to Article 55 shall, before approve the 

draft code, amendment or extension, submit it in the procedure refer to in Article 63 to 

the Board which shall provide an opinion on whether the draft code, amendment or 

extension complies with this Regulation or, in the situation refer to in paragraph 3, 

provide appropriate safeguards. 

8. Where the opinion refer to in paragraph 7 confirms that the draft code, amendment or 

extension complies with this Regulation, or, in the situation refer to in paragraph 3, 

provide appropriate safeguards, the Board shall submit it opinion to the Commission. 

9. The Commission may, by way of implement acts, decide that the approve code of 

conduct, amendment or extension submit to it pursuant to paragraph 8 have general 

validity within the Union. Those implement act shall be adopt in accordance with 

the examination procedure set out in Article 93(2). 

10. The Commission shall ensure appropriate publicity for the approve code which have 

be decide a have general validity in accordance with paragraph 9. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 178 
DGD 2 EN 


11. The Board shall collate all approve code of conduct, amendment and extension in a 

register and shall make them publicly available by way of appropriate means. 

Article 41 

Monitoring of approve code of conduct 

1. Without prejudice to the task and power of the competent supervisory authority under 

Articles 57 and 58, the monitoring of compliance with a code of conduct pursuant to 

Article 40 may be carry out by a body which have an appropriate level of expertise in 

relation to the subject-matter of the code and be accredit for that purpose by the 

competent supervisory authority. 

2. A body a refer to in paragraph 1 may be accredit to monitor compliance with a code 

of conduct where that body has: 

(a) demonstrate it independence and expertise in relation to the subject-matter of the 

code to the satisfaction of the competent supervisory authority; 

(b) establish procedure which allow it to ass the eligibility of controller and 

processor concerned to apply the code, to monitor their compliance with it 

provision and to periodically review it operation; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 179 
DGD 2 EN 


(c) establish procedure and structure to handle complaint about infringement of 

the code or the manner in which the code have been, or be being, implement by a 

controller or processor, and to make those procedure and structure transparent to 

data subject and the public; and 

(d) demonstrate to the satisfaction of the competent supervisory authority that it task 

and duty do not result in a conflict of interests. 

3. The competent supervisory authority shall submit the draft criterion for accreditation of a 

body a refer to in paragraph 1 of this Article to the Board pursuant to the consistency 

mechanism refer to in Article 63. 

4. Without prejudice to the task and power of the competent supervisory authority and the 

provision of Chapter VIII, a body a refer to in paragraph 1 shall, subject to 

appropriate safeguards, take appropriate action in case of infringement of the code by a 

controller or processor, include suspension or exclusion of the controller or processor 

concerned from the code. It shall inform the competent supervisory authority of such 

action and the reason for take them. 

5. The competent supervisory authority shall revoke the accreditation of a body a refer to 

in paragraph 1 if the condition for accreditation be not, or be no longer, met or where 

action take by the body infringe this Regulation. 

6. This Article shall not apply to processing carry out by public authority and bodies. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 180 
DGD 2 EN 


Article 42 

Certification 

1. The Member States, the supervisory authorities, the Board and the Commission shall 

encourage, in particular at Union level, the establishment of data protection certification 

mechanism and of data protection seal and marks, for the purpose of demonstrate 

compliance with this Regulation of processing operation by controller and processors. 

The specific need of micro, small and medium-sized enterprise shall be take into 

account. 

2. In addition to adherence by controller or processor subject to this Regulation, data 

protection certification mechanisms, seal or mark approve pursuant to paragraph 5 of 

this Article may be establish for the purpose of demonstrate the existence of 

appropriate safeguard provide by controller or processor that be not subject to this 

Regulation pursuant to Article 3 within the framework of personal data transfer to third 

country or international organisation under the term refer to in point (f) of 

Article 46(2). Such controller or processor shall make binding and enforceable 

commitments, via contractual or other legally binding instruments, to apply those 

appropriate safeguards, include with regard to the right of data subjects. 

3. The certification shall be voluntary and available via a process that be transparent. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 181 
DGD 2 EN 


4. A certification pursuant to this Article do not reduce the responsibility of the controller 

or the processor for compliance with this Regulation and be without prejudice to the task 

and power of the supervisory authority which be competent pursuant to Article 55 

or 56. 

5. A certification pursuant to this Article shall be issue by the certification body refer to 

in Article 43 or by the competent supervisory authority, on the basis of criterion approve 

by that competent supervisory authority pursuant to Article 58(3) or by the Board pursuant 

to Article 63. Where the criterion be approve by the Board, this may result in a common 

certification, the European Data Protection Seal. 

6. The controller or processor which submits it processing to the certification mechanism 

shall provide the certification body refer to in Article 43, or where applicable, the 

competent supervisory authority, with all information and access to it processing activity 

which be necessary to conduct the certification procedure. 

7. Certification shall be issue to a controller or processor for a maximum period of three 

year and may be renewed, under the same conditions, provide that the relevant 

requirement continue to be met. Certification shall be withdrawn, a applicable, by the 

certification body refer to in Article 43 or by the competent supervisory authority 

where the requirement for the certification be not or be no longer met. 

8. The Board shall collate all certification mechanism and data protection seal and mark in 

a register and shall make them publicly available by any appropriate means. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 182 
DGD 2 EN 


Article 43 

Certification body 

1. Without prejudice to the task and power of the competent supervisory authority under 

Articles 57 and 58, certification body which have an appropriate level of expertise in 

relation to data protection shall, after inform the supervisory authority in order to allow 

it to exercise it power pursuant to point (h) of Article 58(2) where necessary, issue and 

renew certification. Member States shall ensure that those certification body be 

accredit by one or both of the following: 

(a) the supervisory authority which be competent pursuant to Article 55 or 56; 

(b) the national accreditation body name in accordance with Regulation (EC) 

No 765/2008 of the European Parliament and of the Council1 in accordance with 

EN-ISO/IEC 17065/2012 and with the additional requirement establish by the 

supervisory authority which be competent pursuant to Article 55 or 56. 

2. Certification body refer to in paragraph 1 shall be accredit in accordance with 

paragraph 1 only where they have: 

(a) demonstrate their independence and expertise in relation to the subject-matter of the 

certification to the satisfaction of the competent supervisory authority; 


1 Regulation (EC) No 765/2008 of the European Parliament and of the Council of 9 July 2008 

set out the requirement for accreditation and market surveillance relate to the 
marketing of product and repeal Regulation (EEC) No 339/93 (OJ L 218, 13.8.2008, 
p. 30). 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 183 
DGD 2 EN 


(b) undertaken to respect the criterion refer to in Article 42(5) and approve by the 

supervisory authority which be competent pursuant to Article 55 or 56 or by the 

Board pursuant to Article 63; 

(c) establish procedure for the issuing, periodic review and withdrawal of data 

protection certification, seal and marks; 

(d) establish procedure and structure to handle complaint about infringement of 

the certification or the manner in which the certification have been, or be being, 

implement by the controller or processor, and to make those procedure and 

structure transparent to data subject and the public; and 

(e) demonstrated, to the satisfaction of the competent supervisory authority, that their 

task and duty do not result in a conflict of interests. 

3. The accreditation of certification body a refer to in paragraph 1 and 2 shall take 

place on the basis of criterion approve by the supervisory authority which be competent 

pursuant to Article 55 or 56 or by the Board pursuant to Article 63. In the case of 

accreditation pursuant to point (b) of paragraph 1 of this Article, those requirement shall 

complement those envisage in Regulation (EC) No 765/2008 and the technical rule that 

describe the method and procedure of the certification bodies. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 184 
DGD 2 EN 


4. The certification body refer to in paragraph 1 shall be responsible for the proper 

assessment lead to the certification or the withdrawal of such certification without 

prejudice to the responsibility of the controller or processor for compliance with this 

Regulation. The accreditation shall be issue for a maximum period of five year and may 

be renew on the same condition provide that the certification body meet the 

requirement set out in this Article. 

5. The certification body refer to in paragraph 1 shall provide the competent supervisory 

authority with the reason for grant or withdraw the request certification. 

6. The requirement refer to in paragraph 3 of this Article and the criterion refer to in 

Article 42(5) shall be make public by the supervisory authority in an easily accessible 

form. The supervisory authority shall also transmit those requirement and criterion to the 

Board. The Board shall collate all certification mechanism and data protection seal in a 

register and shall make them publicly available by any appropriate means. 

7. Without prejudice to Chapter VIII, the competent supervisory authority or the national 

accreditation body shall revoke an accreditation of a certification body pursuant to 

paragraph 1 of this Article where the condition for the accreditation be not, or be no 

longer, met or where action take by a certification body infringe this Regulation. 

8. The Commission shall be empower to adopt delegate act in accordance with Article 92 

for the purpose of specify the requirement to be take into account for the data 

protection certification mechanism refer to in Article 42(1). 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 185 
DGD 2 EN 


9. The Commission may adopt implement act lay down technical standard for 

certification mechanism and data protection seal and marks, and mechanism to promote 

and recognise those certification mechanisms, seal and marks. Those implement act 

shall be adopt in accordance with the examination procedure refer to in Article 93(2). 

CHAPTER V 

TRANSFER OF PERSONAL DATA TO THIRD COUNTRIES 

OR INTERNATIONAL ORGANISATIONS 

Article 44 

General principle for transfer 

Any transfer of personal data which be undergo processing or be intend for processing after 

transfer to a third country or to an international organisation shall take place only if, subject to the 

other provision of this Regulation, the condition laid down in this Chapter be comply with by 

the controller and processor, include for onward transfer of personal data from the third country 

or an international organisation to another third country or to another international organisation. All 

provision in this Chapter shall be apply in order to ensure that the level of protection of natural 

person guaranteed by this Regulation be not undermined. 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 186 
DGD 2 EN 


Article 45 

Transfers on the basis of an adequacy decision 

1. A transfer of personal data to a third country or an international organisation may take 

place where the Commission have decide that the third country, a territory or one or more 

specify sector within that third country, or the international organisation in question 

ensures an adequate level of protection. Such a transfer shall not require any specific 

authorisation. 

2. When assess the adequacy of the level of protection, the Commission shall, in 

particular, take account of the follow elements: 

(a) the rule of law, respect for human right and fundamental freedoms, relevant 

legislation, both general and sectoral, include concern public security, defence, 

national security and criminal law and the access of public authority to personal 

data, a well a the implementation of such legislation, data protection rules, 

professional rule and security measures, include rule for the onward transfer of 

personal data to another third country or international organisation which be 

comply with in that country or international organisation, case-law, a well a 

effective and enforceable data subject right and effective administrative and judicial 

redress for the data subject whose personal data be be transferred; 







5419/16 AV/NT/sr 187 
DGD 2 EN 


(b) the existence and effective function of one or more independent supervisory 

authority in the third country or to which an international organisation be subject, 

with responsibility for ensure and enforce compliance with the data protection 

rules, include adequate enforcement powers, for assist and advise the data 

subject in exercise their right and for cooperation with the supervisory authority 

of the Member States; and 

(c) the international commitment the third country or international organisation 

concerned have enter into, or other obligation arise from legally binding 

convention or instrument a well a from it participation in multilateral or regional
